Northeast Communications Committee Sends Representatives to Attend Commercial Transport Meeting

▲ Zou En Yuan Passes Through Tianjin to Go South

Shenyang Correspondence: The Ministry of Railways has scheduled to hold a national commercial transport meeting on March 1. Railways across the country and chambers of commerce from various provinces and cities will send representatives to attend and deliberate, with the aim of completing it in ten days. After that, a transport meeting and a national railway intermodal transport meeting will be held for ten days each. The Northeast Communications Committee, having previously received a consultation from the Ministry of Railways, instructed each route to prepare to send representatives to attend. The committee also decided to send Zou En Yuan, the director of the Road Administration Office, to attend and deliberate. Ten routes, including Beining, Hu Hai, Qi Ke, Si Tao, Ji Chang, Tao Ang, Ji Dun, Tao Suo, Ji Hai, and Shen Hai, jointly requested Zou to represent each of these routes in attending. Zou has already departed on the Capital-Beiping-Liaoning Special Express at 12:10 AM on the night of the 23rd. Because Gao Jiyi, the chairman of the committee, went to Tianjin on the 19th, Zou must meet with Chairman Gao in Tianjin to make a request, and plans to stay for one day before going south. It is reported that the Communications Committee has proposed three cases for the commercial transport meeting. The contents are: (1) Regarding the Ministry of Railways' order for each route across the country to increase passenger and freight rates, the Northeast routes have special circumstances and have not increased prices, and are recently preparing to reduce prices to benefit commercial transport and facilitate travel. Railways are public transportation agencies, and their fares must be low and fair, so that the railway business can develop. It is argued that each railway across the country should not increase prices. (2) Railways have never been responsible for the safekeeping of commercial transport goods, and merchants have suffered many losses. Since the Northeast routes implemented responsible transportation of goods, the results have been quite extensive. Each route across the country should uniformly handle this. (3) Merchants are mostly responsible for paying taxes and duties for commercial transport goods, and the railway bureau usually does not intervene, which is inconvenient for merchants. The Northeast routes have long implemented a prepayment method for the formalities of paying taxes and duties for commercial transport goods by the railway bureau, and then collect the amount from each consignee after the goods arrive at the destination. Each route across the country should uniformly handle this. As for the railway transport meeting proposals, there are more than ten cases, most of which are part of the preliminary proposals that the Northeast Communications Committee will soon convene a transport meeting to propose. (February 23)

Eighth Route Army Stationed in Guangxi Returns to Guangdong in Succession

▲ The returnees include Zhang's Brigade and Li's Division

▲ The second batch has arrived in Wuzhou, and the third batch has left Binyang

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the realization of peace in Guangxi, the Eighth Route Army troops have gradually returned to Guangdong. The general situation was seen in yesterday's newspaper. After further investigation, the Eighth Route Army troops are divided into three batches and returned east one after another. The first batch is the First Independent Brigade of Zhang Ruigui's troops and the Huang Zhiwen Brigade of the 126th Division of the 63rd Division of Li Yangjing's troops. The second batch is the Huang Renhuan Brigade of the Training Brigade. The third batch is the 59th Division of Yu Hanmou's troops and the Independent Regiment, etc. Those who have returned east in recent days include the two regiments of Zhang Jingcheng and Wang Yuan of Zhang Ruigui's brigade. After arriving in the province, they went to Shantou to be stationed. On the 19th, Zhong Fangjun's regiment of the brigade and Lin Bin's troops of the Supplementary Regiment of the 126th Brigade of the 63rd Division arrived in the province from Wuzhou. Today (22nd), they boarded the Fuan warship and transferred to Chaoshan. As for the 251st Regiment of Ye Shouyao's troops and the 252nd Regiment of Ouyang Xin's troops under the jurisdiction of Huang Zhiwen of the 126th Brigade of the 63rd Division, they had already arrived in Wuzhou from Tengxian on the 18th. On the 20th, they took dozens of civilian ships and went down the West River, and are expected to arrive in the province today. It is said that after Huang's brigade arrives in the province, it will transfer to Beijiang and be stationed in northern Guangdong with Huang Yanzhen's brigade to consolidate the defense of the area and undertake the work of suppressing bandits in Beijiang. Since the entire division of Division Commander Li is returning to Guangdong, there is no need to establish a division headquarters in Wuzhou, and the troops are ordered to be stationed in Beijiang, so the division headquarters should be moved to Shaoguan to facilitate office work. Deputy Chief of Staff Xu was ordered to quickly end the division headquarters in Wuzhou to facilitate the relocation to Shaoguan. As for the first regiment of Zhang Zhiying's troops, the second regiment of Zeng Youren's troops, and two battalions of Wang Dinghua's troops of the third regiment of Huang Renhuan's brigade of the second batch of returning troops, they also left the Binyang front line on the 14th, arrived in Guixian on the 16th, arrived in Xunzhou on the 19th, and all arrived in Pingnan and Dahuanjiang on the 20th. Today they should be able to arrive in Wuzhou (waiting for ships to return to Guangdong. As for the third batch of returning troops, the Chen Hanguang troops of the Guard Regiment, the Fan Dexing troops of the First Independent Regiment, and the Yu Hanmou troops of the 59th Division, once the Huang Renhuan Brigade returns to the province from Wuzhou, the third batch of troops will return to Wuzhou from Guixun and concentrate for orders. It is estimated that in the future, Yu's division will take the West River of Guangdong as its defense area. (February 21)

Guangdong Province Stops Handling Wuhu Rice and Stone

▲Because the Anhui government levies fees for transporting rice to Guangdong

▲Unanimous Cessation of Transportation Until the Fee is Abolished

Guangzhou Correspondence: The food supply of Guangdong Province has always relied on external sources. Besides ordering rice and stone from Annam and Siam, much of it comes from Wuhu. Therefore, the transportation of Wuhu rice to Guangdong has a very extensive sales route throughout the year, and its price fluctuations have a significant impact on the livelihood of the people of Guangdong. Recently, the Anhui government suddenly announced the collection of passport fees for rice and stone transported to Guangdong, which immediately increased the cost of Wuhu rice. Guangdong rice merchants stationed in Wuhu found it particularly difficult to purchase rice and stone. After receiving a telegram from the Guangdong Rice Merchants' Association, they telegraphed the central government a few days ago, requesting them to order the Anhui government to abolish the passport fees for rice and stone transported to Guangdong as soon as possible, in order to alleviate the merchants' difficulties and maintain the people's food supply. However, recently the Anhui government continued to collect passport fees for rice and stone as before. The Guangdong Rice Bran Distribution Industry Association and the Peanut, Sesame, and Miscellaneous Grains Industry Association specially convened a general meeting to discuss countermeasures. On the 19th, it was resolved to telegraph the central government on one hand, and strictly order the rice merchants' associations in Shantou and Chaoyang, as well as the Ningbo and Yantai rice guilds, to unanimously stop handling Wuhu rice and cease transportation to strive for change. Yesterday, a telegram was sent to the Executive Yuan, which said: "To President Chiang of the Nanjing Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance Song, Anhui Provincial Department of Finance is imposing an exorbitant passport fee on rice and stone exported to Guangdong. We previously received your order to immediately abolish it and strictly prohibit extortion and harassment. However, on the 1st and 2nd of this month, we received a telegram from the Wuhu Guangzhao Public Association stating that the order from the Yuan to stop the rice passport fee was ineffective, and the Anhui authorities are forcibly collecting it with military force at a rate of four jiao per shi. Please vigorously strive for a resolution. This action by the Anhui government is clearly in violation of your order and hinders the people's livelihood. After a joint meeting of our associations, it was resolved to unanimously cease handling the matter to promote awareness. We are sending this telegram for your review and respectfully request that you send personnel to investigate and handle the matter, reiterate the previous order, and strictly order the Anhui government to immediately abolish the rice and stone passport fee, which would be a great blessing for the people's food supply." The Guangdong Rice Bran Distribution Industry Association and the Peanut, Sesame, and Miscellaneous Grains Industry Association respectfully bow and affix their seals. The telegrams sent to the Wuhu Guangdong Rice Guild, and the Shantou, Chaoyang, Ningbo, and Yantai Rice Merchants' Associations, generally stated: "The Anhui Province is defying the central government's orders and forcibly collecting a rice passport fee of four jiao per shi, which is completely unacceptable. The factory associations and others have jointly resolved to unanimously cease handling the matter. Violators will be fined one yuan per package. If your place undermines the joint action, we will never trade with you." (February 22nd)

Qingdao Exempts Inspection Fees for Inland Goods

▲Commodity Inspection Bureau Handles According to Ministry Order

Qingdao Correspondence: Since its establishment, the Qingdao Commodity Inspection Bureau has been collecting inspection fees for all goods, whether exported or sold inland. Because the inspection fees were heavy, merchants in this city once requested the bureau to exempt inspection fees for goods sold inland in order to show consideration, but this request was not granted. As a last resort, the merchants convened a meeting of the Xingzhan Industry Association on the 17th of last month, resolving to telegraph the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, and various party and government agencies in this city, appealing for the exemption of inland inspection fees to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. After receiving the submission, the Ministry of Industry agreed to the request and specially instructed the bureau to comply. After receiving the order, the bureau decided to exempt the fees starting from the 23rd of this month. In addition to posting a notice, they also sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce to forward to various merchants for compliance. The letter to the Chamber of Commerce stated: "According to the Ministry of Industry's Commercial Letter No. 1035, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Qingdao Xingzhan Industry Association have telegraphed one after another, requesting the exemption of inspection fees for goods sold domestically in order to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. Since the merchants have pleaded for hardship, due consideration should be given. You should comply immediately, except for goods that require thorough inspection and those with special circumstances. All goods not for export should be exempt from inspection fees, etc." Upon receiving this order, we must comply. However, the types of goods that should be excluded must be determined by the Ministry. In addition to waiting for the order from the Ministry before instructing the merchants to comply, it is hereby decided to comply with the implementation starting from February 23rd." (February 23rd)

Tragic Fire in Qingdao Slum

▲Spreads to Over Two Hundred Households

▲More Than Two Thousand Refugees

Qingdao Correspondence: The Zangtugou area at the north end of Guanxian Road, Xiling, Qingdao, is where the poor gather. The area is full of one-story wooden houses, built side by side, housing a total of 770 households. At around 1:00 PM today (the 23rd), a fire suddenly broke out. The flames soared into the sky, and the cries of children and women were unbearable to hear. As a result, over 200 houses were burned down, leaving the inhabitants exposed to the elements and awaiting rescue. About 2,000 men, women, children, and elderly were left homeless. The disaster is extremely serious. The cause of the fire is under investigation.

Because the slum's wooden houses were extremely flammable, the Public Security Bureau had planned to ban and order their demolition as a preventative measure. However, due to the onset of winter, they could not bear to leave the poor with no place to live and did not implement the plan. Unexpectedly, at around 1:00 PM on the 23rd, Wei Mingshan, a resident of house number 59, due to making oil and frying fish, the heat was too intense, igniting the oil and spreading to the wooden walls. Moreover, with a strong north wind, the fire became uncontrollable. In less than an hour, more than 200 houses had already been burned down. Fortunately, it was daytime, and men and women had already escaped, so no one was buried in the fire. However, other than the clothes on their backs, they had nothing left, which is truly tragic. When the fire broke out, the Chinese and Japanese fire brigades rushed to the scene upon hearing the news. However, the fire had already become a conflagration, so they did their best to put it out. However, the fire was fierce, and water was scarce. The fire was only slightly subdued by 2:30 PM, and it was not until 4:00 PM that it was extinguished. Afterwards, the Public Security Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau, considering that most of the victims were poor people with no one to rely on, who had suffered this disaster, and were pitiable in the cold and hunger, jointly planned relief measures. They jointly issued a notice that all victims should first register at the Ningbo Guild Hall, and then carefully plan the aftermath based on the number of registered people. In addition, a portion of the empty rooms in Tuandao was allocated to temporarily accommodate the general refugees. According to the investigation, over 200 households have already registered, and about 2,000 people are exposed to the elements without a place to go and urgently need relief. As for whether there were any casualties, it is still under investigation. (February 23rd)

The First Day of the Jiangsu Chambers of Commerce Discussing Business Tax in Zhenjiang

Zhenjiang Correspondence: Representatives from chambers of commerce in various counties of Jiangsu Province gathered at the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce at 3 PM on the 25th to discuss the business tax rates set by the province. Representatives from various counties including Jiading Zhou Yucheng and Zhu Shilin, Baoshan Luodian Wang Yinpan and Jin Yinpei, Gaochun Chen Zicai, Xinghua Zhu Runzhi, Taizhou Jia Hezai and Jia Tongfen, Tongshan Lan Bohua, Jiangdu Wang Jingting, Geng Bo, Hu Yao, Sun Yaozhang and Zhuang Zhongwei, Danyang Guo Songru and Zhou Subo, Longtan Tu Shusan and Lu Shi, Jurong Zhu Jiuxiang and Guo Zhizhong, Jiangyin Yin Zhongren, Yixing Zhu Zhongjing, Cha Jianhou and Wu Lianyin, Wujin Tan Xianglin, Shou Nan, Zhu Yuanpei, Hua Junrong, Cheng Shutze and Lin Junbao, Wujiang Wu Minyu, Peixian Li Wei, Zhenze Xu Ziwei and Yang Gongdu, Shengze Shen Zhiwan, Wuxi Qian Sunqing and Cheng Jingtang, Wuxian Cheng Gan, Huaian Wang Suiliang, Gaoyou Xu Yao, Haimen Yu Xiaochuan, Yancheng Hu Jianchun, Pixian Ren Yushu, Chuansha Cai Jianjiong and Yi Lin Wu Tixian, Jinshan Zhang Yingsan, Jiangpu Lin Chunting, Dongtai Ren Yaofu, and Zhenjiang Lu Xiaobo, Yu Xiaochuan, Hu Jianchun and Zhou Zigeng, totaling 52 representatives from 30 chambers of commerce, were present. Lu Xiaobo and Yu Xiaochuan were elected as temporary chairmen. After the chairmen reported the purpose of the discussion, the proposed agenda was discussed. (1) A proposal by the Wuxi representative to amend Article 4 of the Ministry's promulgated outline and the entire text of Article 8 of the supplementary measures was resolved to be adopted. The chairmen designated Qian Sunqing, Xu Yao, Cheng Ganqing, Zhu Shilin, Zhu Minyu, Tu Shusan, Wang Jingting, Wu Tixian, and Hu Jianchun as the drafting committee, with Qian Sunqing responsible for convening the committee. (2) The representatives from Zhenze and Wujiang proposed that opinions on the special tax rates should be contributed before their promulgation to avoid harming the people. It was resolved that the provincial office should draft the proposal and that merchants' opinions should be collected before the tax rates are promulgated. (3) The proposal to organize a joint provincial chamber of commerce federation was resolved as follows: 1. The provincial office should send a letter to each county's chamber of commerce, inquiring whether they have been reorganized in accordance with the law, and requesting a response before the end of March. 2. The fifteen chambers of commerce that have been reorganized in accordance with the law should take the lead in applying to the Party headquarters for permission to establish a preparatory committee for the provincial chambers of commerce federation meeting. (4) The Wujiang representative proposed to use the proceeds from the sale of treasury bonds by the various customs offices in the province to contribute to the central Party headquarters' construction fund. It was resolved that each county should make donations voluntarily. (5) It was decided that the review of all written opinions would take place at 9:00 AM on the 26th. The drafting committee would also serve as the review committee. In the afternoon, the review report and the opinions of various counties were discussed. The opinions of various counties were summarized as follows: 1. Business tax cannot be levied until all similar miscellaneous taxes are completely abolished. 2. Business tax should not be levied on goods. 3. Business revenue should be based on the original purchase price of goods. 4. Wholesale businesses should be reduced or exempt from tax. 5. The tax rate should be re-determined based on social conditions. 6. Those who have already paid central taxes should be excluded. 7. Following the example of Anhui Province, all tax rates should not exceed two per thousand. 8. Tax collection procedures should be simplified to avoid disturbances. 9. Inland tax rates should not be higher than Shanghai, and the collection period should not be earlier than Shanghai. 10. Chinese and foreign merchants should be taxed equally. 11. Jiangsu Province has not suffered much from the abolition of customs duties, so excessive taxation should not be imposed. 12. The grain, wine, soy sauce, and distilleries industries should be excluded. 13. Silk and satin are not luxury goods and this should be corrected. 14. Handmade cloth should be exempt from tax. 15. Hotels, restaurants, and firecracker businesses have already paid business tax and should be exempt from miscellaneous taxes. 16. The candy, tea, food, and canned goods industries should be exempt from tax. 17. Jewelry and precious stones should be reduced. 18. Pawnshops should be heavily taxed. 19. The money industry should be exempt from business tax. 20. The bundled-tax system should absolutely not be adopted when levying business tax. 21. Opinions on the special tax rate should be contributed before its promulgation to avoid harming the people. 22. The levy of business tax should be uniformly calculated based on the amount of capital.

Provincial Regulations: The detailed rules for the implementation of the Jiangsu Province Business Tax Collection Regulations have been filed with the Ministry and were announced yesterday. It is rumored that the collection regulations have also been revised by the Ministry, but have not yet been announced. Here are some points that have been learned: (1) Those who have been collected special tax by the central government have been deleted. (2) Those who have paid local miscellaneous taxes, such as the wine, dishes, teahouse, hotel, and entertainment venue industries, have also been excluded. (3) The tax rate for jewelry, precious stones, antiques and jade articles, which was originally 20 per thousand, is now changed to 10 per thousand. (4) The insurance industry remains at 20 per thousand. (5) The money industry is levied at 5 per thousand based on the amount of capital. (6) For business tax, if a store also operates other goods, the tax should be levied based on the main part of its business. (7) Wholesale businesses may be levied at half the tax rate. (8) When the collection agency needs to consult the store's books, it must first obtain the consent of the local chamber of commerce. (5) The tax rate is still divided into five levels, namely 1 per thousand, 2 per thousand, 5 per thousand, 10 per thousand, and 20 per thousand. However, most are 2 per thousand. As for the voluntary contribution method of Zhejiang Province, the Finance Department has not yet formally consulted with the representatives. However, the representatives are divided on whether to support or oppose this method. However, regarding the total amount of 4 million yuan, they all believe that whether it is voluntarily contributed or directly collected, it will not be easy to reach the full amount. It is said that the Finance Department estimates that the collection fees for setting up a bureau to collect the tax will also cost hundreds of thousands of yuan each year. If each county can recognize and pay the amount, it may be possible to reduce hundreds of thousands of yuan within the total amount. It is unknown how it will be handled in the future.

The Second Day of the Zhejiang Chamber of Commerce Federation

▲Nomination of Declaration Drafting Committee

The Zhejiang Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation held its first general meeting of members' representatives this morning (the 26th). Fifty-seven people attended. The presidium elected Zhuang Laixian as chairman. Jiang reported that today's meeting would first discuss the draft constitution of the federation, which consists of eleven chapters and a total of sixty-one articles. The secretary-general, Zhu Huiqing, then reported on the preparatory process of the federation. The registration section and investigation section of the provincial chamber of commerce and trade union reported on the work situation of the past ten months. Subsequently, Gu Suming, a member of the presidium, read out the draft constitution, which was discussed, amended, and passed article by article. The meeting adjourned at 12 o'clock. At 3:00 PM, the federation held its second general meeting. The agenda included the election of the Declaration Drafting Committee, discussion of proposals, and various temporary motions. The report of the Proposal Review Committee is recorded below: The committee received a total of 60 proposals by the 25th, most of which related to commercial tax issues. Each proposal was reviewed individually. For the convenience of discussion, the proposals with similar intentions were classified and summarized into 23 items. Other cases were either internal factual issues or unresolved issues that did not fall within the scope of the meeting and should be set aside. The meeting is scheduled to hold elections at 9:00 AM on the 27th, including the election of fifteen executive committee members, seven alternates, seven supervisory committee members, and three alternates (February 26th).

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Ironclad Evidence of Illegal Quarrying at Tianmashan: The case of Jin, wife of Jiang Erchang of Tianmashan, Songjiang County, and stone merchants such as Cao Yunji, continuing to quarry illegally has been repeatedly opposed by local residents and Songjiang natives in Shanghai and Beijing, causing a great uproar. An instruction from the Shatian Bureau when Jiang Erchang applied for the mountain land during his lifetime has now been found, prohibiting quarrying and stipulating that it be used exclusively for Party headquarters public housing and tomb preservation. Now, they are concealing it from the official authorities and secretly quarrying, not donating to build public housing, and even destroying tombs. This is ironclad evidence of illegal mountain opening. The original text is as follows: "Jiangsu Shatian Official Property Affairs Bureau Instruction No. 12, Order to Songjinqing Shatian Branch Bureau, Presentation of a map of Jiang Erchang's application for official land such as Tianmashan for instructions, presentation of the map is fully understood. Jiang Erchang's application for land, according to the original account, is to donate to the Party headquarters for the construction of public housing and the preservation of tombs. It is hereby approved. However, this is to assist the Party headquarters in construction, a special accommodation, and shall not be taken as an example in the future. The recipient must also be notified that quarrying is not allowed. This order, map attached, July 13th, Republic of China 18, Bureau Chief Wu Qiding." Currently, 321 Songjiang natives in Shanghai, including Lei Mingjiu, have submitted a presentation to the Ministry of Finance, requesting the immediate revocation of the license, and have submitted presentations to various agencies requesting that it be permanently closed.

Wuxi

Notorious Bandit from Jiangyin Arrested in Wuxi: Chen Shunfa, a notorious bandit from Jiangyin, participated in the Xia Harbor riots and kidnapped Liu Zijian, a wealthy man from the township, demanding a ransom of 1,650 yuan in May and June of last year. After the case was exposed, he fled to Wuxi and hid under the Taqiao Bridge outside the South Gate. Yesterday, the Third Branch Bureau of Public Security received a secret report and Bureau Chief Wang Weixin took detectives to the address to investigate and arrest him. The bandit Chen was arrested and taken to the bureau. Chen suddenly changed his name to Zhu A'si, hoping to escape punishment, and his confession was vague. The branch bureau prepared a document to send him to the county for interrogation.

Department Order to Ban Huiyuan Steamboat: The Department of Construction previously received a complaint from Yan Dong Steamboat Company accusing the Huiyuan small steamboat of Hui merchants of illegally operating the Hetangqiao route. The Department immediately ordered the Wuxi County Construction Bureau to investigate and verify the matter. After investigation, the bureau found that it was indeed the case and that one license was being used for two purposes, which was inappropriate. Yesterday, they specially notified the steamboat bureau and ordered them to stop operating the Hetangqiao route within three days.

Opening of Agricultural Products Exhibition Hall: The county-run sericulture field, the Education Bureau, the Cooperative Enterprise Guidance Office, and the Nongsang Department's agricultural affairs investigator stationed in Wuxi office, jointly organized the county-wide agricultural products exhibition hall, which held its opening ceremony yesterday (the 26th) at 2:00 PM. Shi Guangyi of the Wuxi water police district, Gu Shuzhi, director of the Agricultural Bank branch, Zhang Renjie and Hu Nianqian of the county Party headquarters, Chen Xianke of the county library, Zhu Zuren of the Yixing Forest Farm, Xue Zilin of the Kunshan Sericulture Field, Zhou Qiwen of the Danyang Sericulture Field, Jiang Chao of the Jiangyin Rural Normal School, Hou Zhenping, representative of the Nongsang Department, and Zhang Pengyuan, along with more than 300 people, attended. County magistrate Pan Zhongjia presided over the meeting and performed the ceremony.

Opening of Investigation Court for Manslaughter Case: Zhou Jingxiao, a member of the Wuxi News Reporters Association, after the tragic death of his wife, Ms. Zhang Shouying, mutually accused Qian, physician, Tao Chishun and his son to the county court. On the 23rd of this month, the court summoned both parties to open the trial and ordered the lawsuit to be suspended in accordance with the law. It is now known that yesterday was the date for the opening of the investigation court, and Prosecutor Zhu summoned the plaintiff Zhou Jing to appear, the defendant Tao Chishun, the witnesses Wu Jiahe, the village security chief of the 14th district, and various doctors related to Zhang's critical situation, Zhang Zaiyang, etc. to appear in court. At 3:00 PM, Judge Zhu opened the court and interrogated Zhou, Tao Chishun, Wu Jiahe, etc. one by one, and then ordered both parties to return to await the verdict.

Shoe Industry Exempt from Business Tax: The Wuxi Shoe Industry Association believes that Jiangsu Province's business tax program has announced that the shoe and hat industry will be taxed at two per thousand. The association says that the shoe and hat industry is a small-scale handmade manufacturing industry, and its raw materials are nothing more than leather, straight tribute, cotton weaving, and silk, all of which have been established separately and taxed separately. If the same industry only collects the raw materials that have been heavily taxed above and then manufactures them by hand, taking a small wage, and then levies business tax, it is no different from adding a bed on top of a bed. The country has a reputation for heavy taxation, and the same industry really has no hope of survival. Therefore, yesterday, they sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce to forward to the Ministry of Finance, the provincial government, and the Department of Finance, to understand the people's livelihood and abolish the collection of business tax in order to maintain the livelihood of handmade industries.

Changzhou

Accelerating the Excavation of the Yunhe and Menghe Rivers: The cost of the project to excavate the Yunhe River and the Menghe River in Wujin County is around 500,000 yuan. Previously, continuous rain and snow greatly affected the progress of the project. Now that the weather is clear, the two river committees have been ordered to accelerate the excavation. All sections of the Yunhe River, except for the section from Shijizui to Guanghua Bridge, the side of the embankment numbered 21, and the area east of Yeshu Town, which are temporarily left out for merchants and drinking water, the remaining sections will be dammed, drained, and excavated immediately. The Menghe River, from Benniu Town to Xiaohe, will be completely dammed and excavated. Starting from the 26th, the two river projects are scheduled to be completed in the shortest possible time.

Two Notorious Bandits Captured in Xiguanzhuang: Xiguanzhuang Village, which connects Wujin County and Jiangyin, is a place where bandits gather. On the 24th, villagers from the Upper District, who had a long-standing feud with the bandits, went to pretend to make peace. The bandits sent two notorious bandits, Xu Genbao and Liu Hongxing, who were carrying box guns, and agreed to negotiate in Huangcun Town. Unexpectedly, the villagers of the Upper District had reported to the provincial guard team stationed at Xiaoxinqiao in advance. When the time came, the two bandits, Xu and Liu, were captured by the guard team, and two box guns and a talisman of the knife society were found. The team escorted the two criminals to the county government for interrogation on the 25th.

Jiangyin

County Consolidation Committee Sends Personnel to Search Bookstores: The Propaganda Department of the County Party Committee Consolidation Committee, in response to a provincial order to ban reactionary publications, specially sent Zhu Tianying to various bookstores on the 24th to investigate. In the Huimin and Huicheng stores, they found "Historical Materialism and Sociology," "Outline of Social Evolution in a Week," "The Moon Breaking Through the Cloud Encirclement," "Revolutionary Biographies of Women in the World," "After Unemployment," "Two Different Kinds of Humans," "Outline of Political Economy," and several obscene novels. They immediately took the books back to the committee. If there were any reactionary remarks, they would be confiscated and destroyed. If there were no reactionary relationships, they would be returned.

Textile Industry Association Holds Meeting to Oppose Customs Duties: The Textile Industry Association believes that the Taixian Hai'an City Textile Industry Association Preparatory Committee has taken the liberty of levying customs duties on textile products from other ports as expenses. It has reported to the Provincial Government Construction Department and the County Party Department to transfer the matter to the province and order the Taixian County Party Department to correct the error. There are also similar cases of levying duties in Dongtai, Yangzhou, Zhenjiang, Changzhou, and other places, which hinder business. Colleagues have repeatedly requested relief from the association. The Executive Committee meeting was held on the 24th and decided that the Industry Association would only collect membership fees from association members. Non-members naturally have no reason to pay fees. The Industry and Commerce Industry Association Law has clear provisions. This illegal levy of duties will not be recognized by the association and should be immediately reported to the province to order the counties to strictly prohibit it, and notify all colleagues. The textile products have already been responsible for the cotton yarn donation, and the Finance Department's draft business tax still has the provisions for the textile industry to pay taxes, which is a kind of double levy. It should be reported to the Ministry of Finance to request that the textile industry tax be eliminated and the county chamber of commerce should be informed to transfer the report.

A Large Gambling Den Raided Outside the North Gate: During the current lunar New Year, gambling in the city is very prevalent. The Public Security First Branch Bureau Chief Cui Siping raided a gambling den in the Jiaotong Hotel outside the North Gate last night and arrested more than 20 people, including lodgers Huang Zuyou (small shopkeeper of Huang Wantong), Cai Laoquan, Ma Lao Si, Fang A'si, Xiao Zhonglin, and teahouse waiter Kong A'wu. Bureau Chief Cui sentenced them to fines of more than one hundred yuan.

Robbery Cases Occur One After Another in Shazhou: Guan Qing, a resident of Lanmensha in the Third District, was kidnapped by bandits the other day and hidden in a house of a certain family in Wushan Port. A bandit was guarding him. Later, Pang took advantage of the bandit's sleepiness and escaped to report to the Zhangjiagang Water Public Security Team. The team was dispatched and four people were arrested. Chen Guoqing's house in Taiziwei was robbed the other night. Fortunately, the family had a self-defense gun to resist, and the robbery failed.

Yangzhou

Major Fire Outside the Deficient Pass City Gate: The area outside the Deficient Pass City Gate and attached to the city is mostly inhabited by poor people such as small vendors and rickshaw pullers. Unexpectedly, at Chou hour (1-3 AM) on the 25th, a fire broke out in the home of a poor man named Chen Liangyu, and it burned along the neighbors Hu Changchun, Zhang Zhineng, Zhang Qixi, and other small households. Fortunately, they were all startled from their dreams and fled independently. Later, the fire was extinguished by the efforts of the fire department. However, the area was a scorched earth, which was a tragic sight. Local philanthropists have raised clothing, food, and reed mats for temporary relief. It is also known that the fire was caused by an argument between the Chen couple, who knocked over a fire pot. They have now fled in fear of punishment.

Scheduled Meeting for National Election: County Magistrate Chen Nanxuan, due to being appointed as the Election Supervisor of Jiangdu County by Hu Pu'an, the Provincial Minister and General Supervisor of the National Assembly Representative Election, ordered the promulgation of the election law, implementation law, and a schedule for various election-related matters to the county. The deadline was set for March 5th to submit the survey groups and election lists to the province. Yesterday (the 24th), a separate letter was sent to various groups, scheduling a meeting in the county on February 26th to plan the implementation, hoping they would attend at the appointed time.

Mistaking Starving People for Bandits at the Sanwenhe River: At dawn on the 25th, Han Wen, the captain of the First Police Company, was informed that there were a large number of bandits looting villages in the town of Sanwenhe, half a li east of the town. He immediately dispatched Zhang, the squad leader of the sub-squad, to lead armed police to the scene. However, the bandits had already left. It was learned that more than 20 starving people from other provinces, who had been transported by boat, had landed on the shore before dawn and begged for food from house to house. The villagers mistook them for bandits and reported to the city. An inspection of the losses revealed that all items were food.

Gaoyou

Continued News of Destroying the Idols of the City God: It is reported that at around 11:00 AM yesterday (the 23rd), eight people wearing suits suddenly came to the City God Temple and destroyed all the idols. It is now learned that the people who destroyed the idols were members of the County Party Headquarters Executive and Supervisory Committee. In order to thoroughly break superstition, the committee members took this action. This morning, the committee members again brought axes and saws to cut the idols of Lord Shen, the City God, and the City God's Wife into several pieces, and hired many laborers to completely throw all the idols of the Twenty-four Departments into the river behind the temple.

Situation After the End of Various Industries' Accounts: The various industries in the county have now completed the closure of last year's accounts in order. Due to the rising gold prices last year, the gold industry and the five-ocean industry have made extremely large profits. Next is the oil, soy sauce, rice and flour industry, whose profits are also not small. As for industries such as money, cloth, and southern goods, due to the impact of last year's poor harvest, business was weak and there was not much profit.

Judicial Investigation into the Warden's Malfeasance at the Detention Center. Jiaxing

Rejection of Fishing Tax Suspension. The Jiaxing County Government, considering the extreme hardship of the fishing households, deemed the collection of fishing tax to be excessively harsh. Therefore, at the 20th County Administrative Meeting, a resolution was passed to petition for the suspension of the tax and to request that the collected taxes from previous years be allocated for warehouse construction expenses. Huzhou

Bandits Rob Two Villages in Succession. In Houzhuang Village, about five li outside the North Gate of the city, over ten bandits speaking with accents from Jiangbei and Henan suddenly broke into the home of Ji Hu Guilian Wang's house late the other night, armed with guns. They stole six bolts of Huasi silk and over ten silver dollars. The owner, Guilian, was injured by the bandits. The bandits then went to the homes of Fei Caifa, Shao Jinfa, Shao Heshang, and Ye Changshou, residents near Gutou, and committed large-scale robberies. Fortunately, the villagers heard the alarm, sounded gongs, and shouted together, causing the bandits to fire several shots and flee north.

Hangzhou

Construction Department Reforms Navigation Administration Methods. Shi Ying, the Director of the Construction Department, after the Provincial Navigation Bureau was merged into divisions and the district sub-bureaus were restored as ship management offices, drafted six reform measures to improve navigation administration. The measures are as follows: (1) More personnel should be dispatched to various docks to inspect and determine the passenger capacity of each ship, avoiding overcrowding to prevent danger. (2) The horsepower of each ship should be limited to no more than 40 horsepower. (3) Each ship should carry a maximum of six towboats. If there are too many passengers, additional trips should be added. (4) Each ship should add men's restrooms for the convenience of passengers. (5) When a ship is about to set sail, it must be inspected by personnel from the office before it can depart. (6) Various forms should be created and distributed to the ships for posting.

Implementation of Joint Defense on the Border of Five Provinces. Previously, the Zhejiang Provincial Government frequently reported border police issues, stemming from bandits being driven from one province to another. Neighboring provinces did not cooperate or communicate, making it impossible to eliminate them permanently. Therefore, joint suppression measures were drafted, stipulating that if a county on the border of two provinces encounters a bandit alarm, troops should be dispatched jointly, regardless of jurisdictional boundaries, without hesitation. These measures were sent to Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Fujian provinces to solicit their agreement. Each province has separately replied, expressing their agreement and requesting a copy of the measures for proper compliance. Chairman Zhang has already sent the sealed measures.

Ningbo

Head of the Anti-Rebel Corps Sent to the Bureau for Investigation. On the 22nd, a young traveler arrived at Room 30 of the Jiaotong Hostel on the north bank of Jiangbei in Ningbo. Dressed in military uniform, he claimed to be Chen Ying, the head of the 2nd Regiment of the Provisional 1st Brigade of the 22nd Division of the Anti-Rebel Army. Yesterday (the 23rd) at 1:00 PM, the traveler suddenly asked the bellboy to send a letter to the 2nd Precinct of the 2nd Sub-Bureau on the north bank of Jiangbei. The letter vaguely stated, "This regiment received 5,000 yuan in pay from Kaifeng and is going to Wufu with two battalions and five companies of soldiers to Yuzhou. Please send a police officer to protect them for three days." Director Yang of the precinct, considering the wording of the letter and the seal on it to be suspicious, invited the adjutant of the 2nd Battalion of the Bao Hong Team to the hostel to question the traveler. The traveler's answers were evasive, and over ten pawn tickets were found. Director Yang and others, considering the traveler's story to be incoherent and likely impersonating a military officer, took the traveler to the precinct and sent a written report to the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Quarrel Between Husband and Wife Leads to Death by Drowning of Uncle and Nephew. In the Wu family of Yizihetou, Zhenhai, lived Jin Ahua, a 30-year-old émigré from Huangyan. He was formerly a soldier but is now unemployed and quarreled with his wife, Xie. Yesterday (the 23rd) afternoon, they quarreled again, and his wife, in a fit of anger, jumped into the Liancao River. Seeing his wife fall into the river, Ahua hurriedly jumped in to rescue her. At that moment, Ahua's maternal uncle, Fa, seeing the situation, also jumped into the river to help. Unexpectedly, because of the continuous rain and snow in the Lian River, the river was very full, resulting in the drowning of both uncle and nephew. Xie was rescued by onlookers and fortunately did not lose her life.

Educational News

Important News

Zhejiang Education Department Petitions the Ministry of Education to Promulgate Regulations for the Certification of Elementary School Teachers

▲ Screening and Reorganizing Teachers

▲ Developing Elementary School Education

The Zhejiang Education Department recently stated that, with the commencement of political tutelage, elementary school education is of utmost importance. To promote the development of elementary school education, the first step is to reorganize elementary school teachers. Since the merger of middle schools and normal schools in 1923, the number of normal school graduates in the province has been small. Currently, nineteen out of ten people working in elementary school education have not received normal school training. Although many of them are excellent talents with educational knowledge and experience, they are limited by their qualifications and cannot fully utilize their strengths. Moreover, unqualified teachers are employed to fill the ranks, while efforts are made to screen and eliminate them, which goes against the state's intention to ensure the efficiency of national education. Furthermore, since 1927, matters related to elementary school education in the province have not been resolved, and the source of normal school graduates is as described above. The difficulty currently felt by those administering local education, apart from funding, is the scarcity of teachers. Although the registration of elementary school teachers separately conducted in the province last year in May was an emergency measure to reorganize elementary school teachers, the results were still difficult to achieve the effect of screening and reorganizing. The Education Department believes that the certification of elementary school teachers is a matter that urgently needs to be addressed. The other day, it specially submitted a document to the Ministry of Education, petitioning for the prompt promulgation of regulations for the certification of elementary school teachers, so that they can be followed and implemented.

Draft of the Outline for the Reorganization of Peiping University

Peiping, 26th. The new organizational outline of Peiping University, drafted by Yin Mo, has been submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval, focusing on unified accounting.

Continued Hearing of the Board of Directors of Jinan University

The Board of Directors of Jinan University held its inaugural meeting the other night at the Jing residence of School Trustee Zhesheng and decided to visit the school for inspection within the next month. The school is currently compiling the minutes.

As reported in the 25th of this newspaper, the articles of association are appended as follows:

▲ Articles of Association of the Board of Directors of National Jinan University

Article 1. The Board of Directors of National Jinan University is established in accordance with the resolution of the Central Executive Committee of the Kuomintang of China, to promote the school and make it the highest institution of learning for overseas Chinese based on the Three Principles of the People. Article 2. The functions and powers of the Board of Directors are as follows: (1) To review and approve the school's construction and improvement plans; (2) To plan the school's endowment fund; (3) To supervise the school's finances; (4) To review and approve the school's regulations; (5) To examine the research of teachers and students on Party ideology and the achievements of each subject; (6) To approve the school's budget and final accounts; (7) To manage the school's property and matters related to purchase and sale; (8) To recommend the school's president to the Ministry of Education for appointment. With regard to the items listed in the aforementioned paragraphs 1, 2, 3, 4, 6, and 7, if they have been discussed and decided by the school's administrative council, the president shall, when submitting them to the Board of Directors, allow relevant personnel designated by the school's administrative council to attend the Board of Directors to explain the content of the proposal. Article 3. The items listed in the aforementioned paragraphs 2, 4, 6, and 7 shall be submitted by the president to the Ministry of Education after being discussed and decided by the Board of Directors. Article 4. The following matters shall be reported by the president to the Board of Directors: (1) Matters related to the appointment and dismissal of teachers and staff; (2) Matters related to curriculum arrangement; (3) Matters related to the assessment of student performance; (4) Matters related to the financial revenue and expenditure; (5) Matters related to the overall statistics of the school. Article 5. If the Board of Directors has opinions on the report in the preceding article, it shall be handled by the president. Article 6. The Board of Directors shall be composed of eleven directors. The directors in the preceding paragraph shall be appointed by the Central Executive Committee. Article 7. The Board of Directors shall elect a managing director from among the directors to handle the affairs of the Board of Directors entrusted by the Board of Directors. Article 8. The Board of Directors shall hold a regular meeting once a month, convened by the managing director. However, in the event of special circumstances, a temporary meeting may be convened by agreement of the managing director or by consultation of three or more directors. Article 9. The meeting of the Board of Directors shall require the attendance of more than half of the directors in Beijing and Shanghai, and its resolutions shall be passed by a majority of those present. Directors who are traveling elsewhere for reasons may be excluded from the calculation, but this shall be recorded in the minutes of the meeting. Directors who are unable to attend for reasons may entrust other directors to represent party comrades, but each director is limited to representing one person. Article 10. When the Board of Directors is in session, one of the managing directors shall be elected as chairman. Article 11. These articles of association shall be submitted to the Central Executive Committee for approval and then submitted to the Ministry of Education for record.

Principals of Various Schools Advocate Drug Prohibition Essay Competition

The 3rd National Drug Prohibition Essay Competition for Students in Universities and Middle Schools has been prepared for many days by the Education Section of the China National Drug Prohibition Association and is now ready. Letters requesting the rules are pouring in from various places. It is heard that the deadline for registration is set for April 1st of this year, and the deadline for submission of manuscripts is set for May 1st. This extended period is intended to make the event accessible throughout the country, so that students in remote areas may have the opportunity to participate. The Association also intends to promote the event widely by directly writing to the principals of major universities and middle schools across the country, urging them to announce the event to their students and encourage them to register actively. It is heard that over 5,000 of these letters have been sent. As of yesterday, they have been sent to major universities and middle schools in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangxi provinces. They are now planning to send them to Fujian, Guangdong, Guangxi, and other provinces, and then to provinces north of the Yangtze River. The letter to the principals of major universities and middle schools across the country reads as follows: "Dear Sir/Madam, In order to promote drug prohibition education, our Association has held national drug prohibition essay competitions for students in previous years. Many brilliant works have been produced, greatly influencing society. This year, we plan to hold the event on a larger scale, so that students throughout the country can express their great views and win prizes, setting a new record in the history of drug prohibition. We have long admired your deep hatred for the flow of opium and narcotics and your unwavering efforts to promote drug prohibition education. We are now sending you the rules and registration forms and sincerely hope that you will immediately announce the event and encourage your students to register and participate in this grand event. We eagerly await your response." It is said that the regulations will be sent immediately upon request.

First Preparatory Meeting of the County Social Education Research Association

The Yutang Public Education Center in Shanghai County and other social education organizations, in order to study the implementation methods of public education and expand public education promotion, have jointly organized a Social Education Research Association. The first preparatory meeting was held at the Minhang Public Education Center yesterday afternoon. Over ten people attended, including Rui Chi from the Yutang Public Education Center, Zhang Fengshan from the County Agricultural Education Center, Zhang Jingye from the County Library, and Jin Zuo Bin and Xi Langqing from the County Public Education Center. After the formalities, the purpose of the meeting was reported, followed by a discussion: (1) Regarding the name of the association, it was resolved that it would be the Shanghai County Social Education Research Association; (2) Regarding the purpose of the association, it was resolved that the association would study the theory and methods of public education based on the spirit of mutual assistance and cooperation, and promote them; (3) Regarding the determination of members, it was resolved to divide them into three types: basic, ordinary, and special. (1) The public education centers, agricultural education centers, libraries, gymnasiums, and experimental farms in the county would be basic members; (2) Other social education organizations in the county may become ordinary members with the recommendation of the basic members of the association; (3) Those who study social education may be hired as special members of the association; (4) Regarding the organization of the association, it was resolved to divide it into three sections: general affairs, research, and promotion. General affairs is divided into three sections: documentation, accounting, and general affairs. Research is divided into three sections: investigation, editing, and statistics. Promotion is divided into two sections: public relations and publicity; (4) Regarding the determination of meeting dates, it was resolved that the first Thursday of each month would be the date of the association's regular meeting, and temporary meetings could be convened when necessary; (6) Regarding the association's funding, it was resolved that basic members would contribute fifteen per thousand of their respective organizations' funding, and ordinary members would contribute half a yuan every six months; (7) Regarding the location of the association, it was resolved that it would be the Minhang Public Education Center; (8) Nomination of Drafting Committee members, it was resolved that, the Yutang Public Education Center, the County Library, and the local library would be nominated; (7) The date for the second preparatory meeting was decided as follows; After the discussion, the meeting was adjourned.

Establishment of Fahua Middle School in Fahua District

Yang Yongxing and other administrative committee members of the Fahua District in western Shanghai believe that the district is close to the concessions, densely populated, and has a growing number of young students. However, the district only has elementary schools, and many poor students are forced to discontinue their education due to lack of funds to attend higher schools. As a result, many students are unable to receive further education. Therefore, it is necessary to immediately establish a middle school, provide comprehensive facilities, and reduce tuition fees, so that local students can continue their education. Therefore, Mr. Yang invited local residents the other day to discuss the implementation plans. As a result, it was decided that the school would be built on public land such as the Jiji Warehouse and Fahua Temple in Fahua Town, and the funds would be raised from the land and the district office. Everything is generally in place. The name has also been decided as Fahua Middle School. Priority will be given to local students, and the remaining places will be open to others. It has also been decided to start preparations immediately, in the hope of establishing the school as soon as possible.

The entrance examination for new students at China Public School this semester has not yet been announced, and unrest has occurred within the school. Now that the school's reorganization is complete, prospective students are inquiring at the school. The school hereby issues the following notice: Notice: The entrance examination for new students this semester has been delayed due to a special event at the school, and the results have not yet been announced. Now that the school's reorganization is complete, the entrance examination work is being expedited. The results will be announced soon. For students who did not pass the entrance examination, considering the delay caused by the special event at the school, which prevented them from taking examinations at other schools, it is planned to enroll them all as special students. They will be admitted as special students and will be converted to regular students in the future after passing the examination and meeting the qualification requirements according to Article 7 of the school's regulations. Please note. This notice is hereby given.

Shanghai Basketball Association Yesterday's Match: Chi Zhi Loses to Zhenru by One Point

丨Result: 21 to 29丨

▲ You Ai Wins You Ai 29 to 16

▲ Yao Guang Wins Tu Jin 34 to 28

▲ Qing Guang Wins Tongji 35 to 28

In last night's Shanghai Basketball Association's four-group matches, the Zhenru vs. Chi Zhi game was exceptionally fierce. Chi Zhi led 21 to 10 in the first half, but ultimately lost to Zhenru by one point. The overall results of the four groups are as follows: (1) You Ai wins San San 29 to 16; (2) Yao Guang wins Guo Jin, 34 to 38; (3) Qing Guang wins Tongji 35 to 28; (4) Zhenru wins Chi Zhi 29 to 28.

▲ Qing Guang Wins Tongji (Group A)

The game started at 7:30 PM. The tension between the two teams was high. Qing Guang consistently maintained a slight lead from the beginning, but the scores remained close. They were tied at 11-11 at one point. Tan Da scored a free throw, giving Qing Guang a 12-11 lead at halftime. Tongji scored first in the second half, tying the score at 10, but failed to surpass Qing Guang. Qing Guang then regained the upper hand. Tongji's Ji Yubiao scored twice, narrowing the gap to 18-19, just one point behind Qing Guang. Victory seemed within reach, but the defense faltered, and Qing Guang seized the opportunity, leading all the way to a 34-28 victory over Tongji. The highest scorer for both teams was Tongji's Ji Yubiao, who scored 18 points, truly a key contributor.

▲ Zhenru Wins Chi Zhi (Group A)

In the first half, Chi Zhi had a smooth run. Qian Dingzhen and Yang Yulin's long-range shots were incredibly accurate, earning applause from the spectators and scoring a total of 21 points. Zhenru struggled and only scored 10 points. However, from the second half onwards, Zhenru's momentum suddenly surged. Cai Rongrui scored again, securing the victory. In this thrilling match, Zhenru defeated Chi Zhi 29-28, a fortunate outcome indeed.

Shandong Prepares for the North China Games

▲ Drafting the General Outline of the Organizing Committee

▲ Expanding the Stadium Construction

▲ Opening Tennis and Baseball Fields

▲ Hiring Registered Preliminary Contest Personnel

Jinan Correspondence: The 15th North China Games have been decided to be held in Jinan this year. The province has established the Shandong Organizing Committee for the 15th North China Games, responsible for handling the affairs. This afternoon (the 23rd) at 4:00 PM, the committee held its first meeting at the Public Sports Field outside Nanweimen. Committee members He Siyuan, Zhang Yue, Zhang Weicun, Zhang Hongjian, Zhang Honglie, and Wang Xiang attended. Attendees included Yang Peng, a clerk from the Department of Education, Pi Songyun, the head of the Third Section, Zhang Hongwen, the director of the Jinan Municipal Engineering Bureau, Zhang Yixian, the director of the Sports Field, and Tong Jinbiao, the instructor of the Sports Field. He Siyuan chaired the meeting, and Yang Peng took the minutes. The meeting began with a report from the chairman, stating that the 15th North China Games would be held in Shandong this year, with participants from twelve provinces and three municipalities. As the host, Shandong should prepare thoroughly. The previous games were held in Nanjing, with Nanjing's budget reaching 300,000 yuan. Shandong should pay attention to this. As the deadline approaches, preparations for the games and funding must be made in advance. Then, discussions began: (1) Regarding the organization of the North China Games, it was decided to have Committee Member He Siyuan draft a general outline for review. (2) Regarding the stadium, the chairman first asked Zhang Yixian, the director of the Public Sports Field, to explain the layout of the field. The 12th Games were held in Shandong at the Public Sports Field, which covers 54 mu. It was felt that the terrain was unfavorable, being lower in the northwest and higher in the southeast. The straight track, which is 220 meters long, was also considered insufficient. The 12th Games had 40 participating groups, and this time, the number of participating groups would double. The facilities within the field are inadequate. The viewing stands for the 12th Games were made of straw mats, which was uneconomical. This year's games must be prepared thoroughly, and the venue is also the location for Jinan's public sports activities, so it is even more appropriate to make long-term plans. (A) Leveling the terrain. (B) Extending the straight track to 270-280 meters and reducing the angle of the 400-meter circular track. (C) Constructing viewing stands to accommodate 15,000 people, with three people per two meters. (D) Constructing a viewing stand in the middle of the east side of the straight track for officials and important guests. (E) Adding buildings for storing sports equipment and for use as offices. (F) Opening tennis, baseball, and team ball fields on the newly purchased 11 mu of land (east of the existing venue) for this year's games and future use. (G) Constructing a shelter from wind and rain, for future use. (H) Digging wells. It was decided to construct viewing stands for 30,000 people, and other construction matters would be handled jointly by the Construction Department, the Engineering Bureau, and the Sports Field. They would begin surveying and measuring tomorrow and then design and estimate the costs, aiming to complete everything before the games begin. (3) Regarding the funding of the games, it was decided that the committees would prepare budgets and submit them to the provincial government for discussion. The funding for the games would be submitted to the central government, and letters would be sent to various provinces and municipalities in North China for donations. (4) Regarding sports talent, it was decided that the organizing committee would register officials for track and field events and hire sports experts from Beijing to serve. The meeting adjourned. It is reported that the Provincial Public Sports Field is located outside Nanweimen, at the foot of Thousand Buddha Mountain. West from Nanweimen, there is a main road leading to Thousand Buddha Mountain. East from Xinxinzhen and Nanweimen, there is a main road leading to Kaiyuan Temple. The original field covers 54 mu, is long from north to south, and narrow from east to west. The office buildings are located in the northeast corner of the field. West of the building is the tennis court. In front of the gate is the first basketball court, and south of that are the second and third basketball courts. West of these is the track, with the field events area in the middle (used for both soccer and football). The newly purchased 11 mu of land to the east of the field will be used to open tennis, baseball, and team ball fields. A shelter from wind and rain will be built in the northwest corner, and wells will be dug. Once completed, it will be a magnificent sight. It is also reported that Provincial Chairman Han Fuqu ordered the Municipal Engineering Bureau to repair the roads leading to Thousand Buddha Mountain and Kaiyuan Temple before the games so that athletes from various provinces could visit the scenic spots. This is also a noteworthy part of the preparations for the North China Games.

The Fourth Champagne Cup Tournament

▲ Competition Starts on Sunday, March 1st

▲ Details of the Representatives' Meeting

The long-awaited Shanghai Race Club's Fourth Table Tennis Champagne Cup Tournament is actively being prepared and is scheduled to begin on March 1st. The competition schedule for each group has also been released by the tournament organizing committee. With this declaration of war issued, athletes from various teams are sharpening their weapons and preparing for fierce competition.

The representatives' meeting for all teams participating in the tournament on the evening of the 25th was held as scheduled. The resolutions are as follows: (1) The competition will use Double Happiness brand table tennis balls. (2) If Team A wishes to postpone a match with Team B, they may directly contact the opposing team and must report to the organizing committee. The match must be rescheduled within two weeks. If the opposing team does not agree to the postponement, the original schedule will be followed. (3) Jiaotong University requested a group competition format. The majority decided to continue with a single round-robin format to promote participation and comply with the regulations. (4) The competition will be held at seven locations: the Race Club, China Trust, Shanghai Cloth, Tongyi, G.A., Qibu, and Hongle. (5) If Team A is unable to arrive on time due to unforeseen circumstances, the opposing team may grant a grace period. If a grace period is not granted, Team A may report the details to the organizing committee, which will make a decision based on the situation. (6) Competition results must be submitted within two days of the match. Do not follow the example of the former G.A. Cup, etc., in delaying the submission. (7) Rules for table tennis matches in foreign countries will be used. (8) Tea and snacks were served at the end of the meeting.
