Commercial News: Financial and Gold Markets Continue Upward Trend

▲ The Atmosphere Dictates…Utter Chaos

▲ Changes Appear Constantly

Yesterday, February 26th, the bid price for gold continued to rise. The market situation was unpredictable and unstable. The danger of the waves was ultimately unavoidable and was truly controlled by the environmental atmosphere. People's minds were extremely confused. There were changes of fifteen or sixteen taels in both the morning and afternoon markets. As for foreign exchange, it strengthened and then weakened, eventually trending firmly. The listed price continued to narrow by one and a half notches. Overseas silver markets all fell, so the gold price opened high, and various firms were very hesitant to buy and sell. Firms such as Qian Changxiang, Chang Sheng Yong, etc., sold and then bought back. Yuan Mao, Yong Yuanheng, Yuanheng, and Cheng Yuan, etc., all had purchases. The Dalian gang, Tong Taichang, etc., all issued positions. Later, the market weakened from strong. It fell from 780 taels to within 70 taels, because the exchange rate turned weak, and large households sold off. And the Bank of England initially took one shilling and two pence one eight seven five, but later rose to two pence four three seven five. Until noon, speculators suddenly re-entered, and in an instant, the situation changed. The exchange rate stabilized, suddenly showing a strong upward trend, breaking through the 80-tael mark again, which was truly a meaningless move. The afternoon market initially seemed sharp, reaching 790 taels. Later, the Indian exchange rate reported an increase, and there were widespread rumors that a large amount of cash was being exported. Unexpectedly, there was no movement at all, which was truly due to the effect of the atmosphere. Therefore, people's minds turned downward, and there was a sharp drop of more than ten taels. The final calculation was 75 or 76 taels, and the cashiers of various firms were divided. As for spot goods, an additional six taels must be added. Is the forecast for the large strip to be lower again this morning?

▲ High Opening

From the opening of the April market in the morning, it rose by four taels and seven mace, to 773 taels and five mace, because the large strip did indeed fall by five sixteenths, and the silver price fell by one-half. Yarn and Cotton: Yarn Market Initially High and Then Low

The yarn market initially rose and then fell. The speed of changes in recent days has made it difficult for people to grasp. However, a certain industrialist has a very strong sense of high-level thinking, because cotton is difficult to loosen, and there is no hope for a turnaround in exchange rates. Indian cotton is becoming increasingly difficult to import, so most of the long positions are held tightly and not released. However, the current yarn sales are quite sluggish, and various gangs are lifeless. According to one part, the price is too high, so sales are sluggish. However, the period is currently the peak season in spring, and there is still hope for development. It is difficult to predict what the future holds. In short, it must depend on the amount of demand and raw materials for advancement and retreat.

▲ Human Bids Return Soft

The human bid market opened in the morning, and because the gold price was high and the foreign cotton was rising, the market atmosphere was tight, and each rose by one or two taels and eight or nine qian. In the second and third markets, the price turned down due to a lack of buyers. As a result, each month's bids rose by two, three, or four qian, but large households still entered. The market opened firmly again in the afternoon, rising by eight or nine qian. The second and third markets fell slightly because the raw cotton was slightly weak, and each month fell by two taels and four qian to one tael and three, four, or five qian. The total transactions for the day were 25,800 bales. Cotton Market Situation Slightly Soft

The cotton market trend is slightly weak, but Indian cotton is still rising fiercely, and the exchange rate has shrunk greatly, so there is a great upward force. In fact, it had already risen sharply on the previous day, and most of the retail short sellers cut their losses and liquidated, so there was a lack of buyers in the market. Generally cautious people see the recent ups and downs and dare not move. Only Japanese merchants have a slight intention to sell, but they are still spreading air in the market. In short, once the price is high, those outside the industry are helpless. Most buyers have to look at 50 taels. However, the current cotton procurement by various factories is very sluggish, because the yarn sales are not good.

The Shanghai County Reorganization Committee Uncovers a Major Gambling Den in Sanlintang

As the old lunar year ends, bad habits spring up in the countryside, especially gambling. A group of unemployed vagrants gather to gamble and skim profits, treating it as a profession. The Shanghai County Reorganization Committee, in order to eliminate this bad habit, has repeatedly put forward suggestions and handed them over to the County Public Security Bureau for execution, and also sent personnel to inspect various districts in person. Unexpectedly, yesterday the committee learned that a major "yao tan" gambling game was being played overnight in the Sanlintang Qigan Street Club, lasting all night and being completely unbridled. Therefore, members of the committee secretly went to the gambling venue late at night to investigate the truth. Immediately, they joined forces with Zhang, the bureau chief of the Fourth Branch of the County Public Security Bureau, leading many police officers, and successively captured forty-eight gamblers. They also seized gambling equipment and gambling funds, and brought them all to the bureau. After Bureau Chief Zhang interrogated the gamblers one by one, he meted out punishments separately. It is reported that the branch bureau has reported the details of the crackdown to the County Reorganization Committee, and the committee has resolved to send a letter to the County Government ordering the Public Security Bureau to thoroughly investigate the main criminals in the case in order to prevent a recurrence.

Three People Die Tragically

▲ Found Dead: Yesterday (the 26th) morning at 7 a.m., a male corpse was found lying dead at the end of the back alley of the Beishun Zangli in Xinmin Road, Zhabei. He was about forty years old, with a long face, wearing a dark blue imitation straight tribute wool, an old cotton robe, gray cloth cotton pants, bareheaded and barefoot. Wang Shutong, a policeman from post number 17 of the first precinct of the fourth district, found the body, reported to the station chief, and immediately ordered the neighborhood head to report to the local court. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Zhao Zikui was dispatched, accompanied by clerks and police officers, to the scene. After examination, it was confirmed that he had died of illness. As no family members were found, the neighborhood head was instructed to collect a coffin from the charity hall for burial in the public cemetery pending verification.

▲ Fell to Death: Carpenter Wang Zonggen, 24 years old, from Pudong, residing at 300 Qipu Road, yesterday morning at 10:30 a.m. was working on the new Western-style prison on Huade Road. Accidentally, he fell from the seventh floor. His head was split open, and blood flowed from his abdomen. He died instantly. The construction contractor reported to the Tilamqiao Police Station, which ordered Hua Bu number 1815 to come to the scene. The body was taken by vehicle to Tongren Hospital, and then to the coroner's office to await examination.

▲ Crushed to Death: An old woman, surname unknown, about fifty or sixty years old, resembling a female servant,

Yesterday at about 2:15 p.m., she was walking through the intersection of North Zhejiang Road when she was suddenly hit by tram number 48 on Route 6 heading north to the train station. Unable to avoid it, she was knocked to the ground, breaking her skull and left leg, and causing her large intestine to bleed. She died instantly. Hua Bu number 2677 was then dispatched to arrest [the driver] and transport the body to Tongren Hospital for examination at the coroner's office.

Fire Broke Out in Yangjiazhai the Night Before Last

At 12 o'clock the night before last, a fire suddenly broke out at the home of Shandong resident Lü Xinmai near the Tuditang in Yangjiazhai, Pudong. The fire was fierce and unapproachable. The fire brigade drove to the scene and put out the fire with water. A total of four and a half bungalows were destroyed. Afterwards, the police of the Fourth Squad of the Police Department ordered the police to transfer Lü to the Third District of the Public Security Bureau to investigate the cause of the fire for verification.

Golden Theater to Screen Swordsmen Feature Film

In the early days of American film development, a type of swordsmen and detective feature film was popular, such as "The Adventures of Bao Lian" and "The Black Hand Gang." Those with a silver screen habit can still talk about their merits. As love short films became popular, swordsmen feature films were temporarily eliminated. In fact, this type of feature film is the most difficult to produce, and the compact plot and serious acting are most likely to excite emotions and boost morale. The owner of the Golden Grand Theater, in view of this, specially ordered a variety of the latest swordsmen detective feature films from the United States. The most recently arrived is the complete series of "The Green Forest Monster." The plot twists and turns, the thrilling fights, and the mysterious mechanisms of the film are compact and amazing in every episode, without the shortcomings of current films that are all about flesh and boring love stories. It is said that the film will be released to the public soon.
